There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\\n514:         // the split doesn't happen too often.\\n515:         CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\\n516:                                                 Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\\n517:         Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\\n518:         int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\\n519:         Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\\n520:         while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\\n521:             ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\\n522:             incomplete.add(batch);\\n523:             // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\\n524:             synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\\n525:                 if (transactionManager != null) {\\n526:                     // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\\n527:                     transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\\n528:                     insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\\n529:                 } else {\\n530:                     partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\\n531:                 }\\n532:             }\\n533:         }\\n534:         return numSplitBatches;\\n535:     }\\n536: \\n537:     // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\\n538:     // multiple requests in flight to that partition. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\\n546:     // IllegalStateException instead.\\n547:     private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\\n548:         // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\\n549:         if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\\n550:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \\\" +\\n551:                 \\\"though idempotency is enabled.\\\");\\n552: \\n553:         if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\\n554:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \\\" +\\n555:                 \\\"requests. batch.topicPartition: \\\" + batch.topicPartition + \\\";
